<p>Dutchification of older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bacterium</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">bactērium</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">βακτήριον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">baktḗrion</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">small staff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">βακτηρία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">baktēría</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bacterie.html>bacterie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bacterie.html>bacteriën</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bacterie.html>bacterietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***badkamer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:badkamer.html>badkamer</a> (1999)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bad</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamer</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:badkamer.html>badkamer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:badkamers.html>badkamers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:badkamer.html>badkamertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bathroom</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In English, <i>bathroom</i> may mean a room with only a <a href = vnd.unilang:toilet.html>toilet</a>, but <i><a href = vnd.unilang:badkamer.html>badkamer</a></i> always refers to a room with a bath and/or a shower (and possibly a <a href = vnd.unilang:toilet.html>toilet</a>).
</p>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdachte.html>verdachte</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bagatelliseren.html>bagatelliseerde</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gevaar.html>gevaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontstaan.html>ontstaan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>toen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> machinegeweermagazijn leegschoot <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:openbare.html>openbare</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weg.html>weg</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The suspect <b>trivialised</b> the danger that could have arisen when he emptied the magazine of a machine gun on a public road.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***bagger.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bagger.html>bagger</a> (20145)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bagger.html>bagger</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>mud, dredge, dirt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:varkens.html>varkens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wroeten.html>wroeten</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bagger.html>bagger</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The pigs are rooting in the <b>mud</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>filth, muck, any mucky or dirty substance (such as dredge)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> junk, crap, stuff <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">substandard <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

***bak.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bak.html>bak</a> (1635)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">bac</i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bak.html>bak</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakken.html>bakken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakje.html>bakje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a container, such as a box, a crate, a tray or a tub</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a drinking vessel, usually a cup or mug</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a vehicle, a car</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bak.html>bak</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">first-person singular present indicative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakken.html>bakken</a></i></span></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">  imperative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakken.html>bakken</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">*<a href = vnd.unilang:bak.html>bak</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bake</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">baec</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">meat from the back of a pig</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:bak.html>bak</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">back, rear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*baką</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">back</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is"><a href = vnd.unilang:bak.html>bak</a></i>. Etymologically related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakboord.html>bakboord</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:achterbaks.html>achterbaks</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bak.html>bak</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakken.html>bakken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakje.html>bakje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>pork: the meat of a pig</li>
<li>a pig</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to quarrel, to argue, to fight [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></i> <span>(about/<a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>)</span></span>] <span class="defdate">[from 18th c.]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fight, to brawl <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to engage in physical combat</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> <span class="defdate">[late 17th <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> 20th c.]</span></li></ol>

***bakken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bakken.html>bakken</a> (4182)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">backen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:baken.html>baken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bakkan</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bakan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bakaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰeh₃g-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakken.html>bakken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ergative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bake</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ergative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pan-fry</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">pan-fry</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> The distinction between <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bakken.html>bakken</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:braden.html>braden</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> somewhat unclear and depending on idiolect. The general word for pan-frying <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bakken.html>bakken</a></i>, but <i><a href = vnd.unilang:braden.html>braden</a></i> may alternatively be used with meat. Many <a href = vnd.unilang:speakers.html>speakers</a> use <i><a href = vnd.unilang:braden.html>braden</a></i> chiefly in the sense of “to roast, to grill”.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bakker.html>bakker</a> (9288)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">backer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bakar</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*baker</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bakārijaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakker.html>bakker</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakkers.html>bakkers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakker.html>bakkertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">bakster</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">bakkerin</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>baker (person who bakes and sells bread, etc)</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:beroep.html>beroep</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brood.html>brood</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:taarten.html>taarten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bakt.html>bakt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verkopen.html>verkopen</a>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bakkerij.html>bakkerij</a> (12953)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakken.html>bakken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-erij</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ery</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Or alternatively, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakker.html>bakker</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">baker</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ij</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-y</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also the usage notes at <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-erij</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bakery</i>, and German and Luxembourgish <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bäckerei</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bakery</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***bakvis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bakvis.html>bakvis</a> (66010)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakken.html>bakken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bake, fry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vis.html>vis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The sense “teenage girl” <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Backfisch</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakvis.html>bakvis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakvissen.html>bakvissen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakvisje.html>bakvisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A pubescent girl, connoting giggliness and fangirlism.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A fish cooked by frying (rather then boiling etc.), referring either a culinary dish or a species usually thus prepared.
<ul><li><b>1863</b>, von Ehrenkreutz, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:liefhebber.html>liefhebber</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hengelen.html>hengelen</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:volledig.html>Volledig</a> handboek ten <a href = vnd.unilang:dienste.html>dienste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hengelaars.html>hengelaars</a></i>, tr. from German, H. C. A. <a href = vnd.unilang:campagne.html>Campagne</a> (publ.), page 82.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> [<a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Hesseling] <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gezonde.html>gezonde</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vooral.html>vooral</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goede.html>goede</a> <b>bakvisch</b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bal.html>bal</a> (943)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bal.html>bal</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:bal.html>bal</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*balluz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bal.html>bal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ballen.html>ballen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:balletje.html>balletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a ball or any object with such a shape</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> testicle, <a href = vnd.unilang:nut.html>nut</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pass, shot
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>Lekker</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:balletje.html>balletje</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Nice pass/shot!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">toff</span>, posh person</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:bal.html>bal</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ballare</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bal.html>bal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bals.html>bals</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:balletje.html>balletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>ball, dance party</li></ol>

<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>

***baldrick.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:baldrick.html>baldrick</a> (12568)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:baldrick.html>baldrick</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">baldricks</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A broad <a href = vnd.unilang:belt.html>belt</a>, sometimes richly ornamented, worn <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> one shoulder, across the breast, and under the opposite arm; less properly, any <a href = vnd.unilang:belt.html>belt</a>.
<ul><li><b>1400?</b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a> Gawain and the Green Knight</i>, line 2485.:
<dl><dd>And the bright green <a href = vnd.unilang:belt.html>belt</a> on his body he bore, oblique, like a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:baldrick.html>baldrick</a></b>, bound at his side below his left shoulder, laced in a knot...</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1598</b>, William Shakespeare, <i>Much Ado About Nothing</i>, Act I, Scene I, line 238:
<dl><dd>That a woman conceiv'd <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>, I thank her; that she <a href = vnd.unilang:brought.html>brought</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> up, I likewise give her most humble <a href = vnd.unilang:thanks.html>thanks</a>; but that I will have a rechate winded in my forehead, or hang my <a href = vnd.unilang:bugle.html>bugle</a> in an invisible <b><a href = vnd.unilang:baldrick.html>baldrick</a></b>, all women shall <a href = vnd.unilang:pardon.html>pardon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1800?</b>, Alfred, Lord Tennyson, <i>The Lady Of Shalott</i>, part III, verse 2:
<dl><dd>And from his blazoned <b><a href = vnd.unilang:baldrick.html>baldrick</a></b> slung, a mighty silver <a href = vnd.unilang:bugle.html>bugle</a> hung...</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1786</b>,  Francis Grose,  <cite>A Treatise on Ancient Armour and <a href = vnd.unilang:weapons.html>Weapons</a></cite>, page 33:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The sword <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> carried in a <a href = vnd.unilang:belt.html>belt</a> of buff or other leather girded round the body, or thrown <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the right shoulder, these shoulder belts <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> called <b>baudricks</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">balaena</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">whale</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">φάλαινα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">phálaina</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">whale</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">baleen</i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>(type of material) baleen
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baard.html>baard</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">walvisbeen</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li>a whalebone; a baleen</li>
<li>a <a href = vnd.unilang:spoken.html>spoke</a> that reinforces an umbrella or <a href = vnd.unilang:parasol.html>parasol</a> (in the past often made of baleen)</li></ol>

***balken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:balken.html>balken</a> (19927)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:balken.html>balken</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">belken</i>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bulken.html>bulken</a></i>, probably onomatopoeic. Similar formations are found in <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">bölken</i> (from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span></span>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:balk.html>balkje</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">belch</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:balken.html>balken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bray, make a donkey's sound</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to utter asinine talk</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bawl, cry, weep loudly</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <a href = vnd.unilang:belt.html>belt</a>, sing loudly</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ballon.html>ballon</a> (7611)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:ballon.html>ballon</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. ***balpen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:balpen.html>balpen</a> (32799)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bal.html>bal</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ball</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pen.html>pen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:pen.html>pen</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ball <a href = vnd.unilang:pen.html>pen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:balsemen.html>balsemen</a> (44130)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">balsamen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:balsem.html>balsem</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:balsemen.html>balsemen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to embalm, treat a corpse in order to prevent decomposition long-term</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to treat with a balm</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to soften, physically or emotionally</li></ol>
